### [1] [Hybrid Quantum-Classical Detection for RIS-Assisted SC-FDE via Grover Adaptive Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04173)
*Maryam Tariq,Omar Alhussein,Raneem Abdelraheem,Abdullah Quran,Georges Kaddoum,Sami Muhaidat*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 把ML检测转为QUBO并用Grover自适应搜索解决，辅以频域MMSE初始化，既能在理想量子条件下接近最优又享有平方加速；在噪声下通过低深度电路和初始化仍能保持接近MMSE的性能，表明量子增强检测在RIS辅助6G宽带通信中可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 6G对宽带和低延迟检测器提出高性能且不指数复杂度的需求，RIS辅助SC-FDE在频选择性信道下的高复杂度ML检测亟需有效的近似或加速方法，量子算法（如GAS）提供潜在的次指数加速。

Method: 将SC-FDE的ML检测目标转为QUBO格式，采用Grover自适应搜索（GAS）量子算法求解；引入基于循环结构的频域MMSE阈值用于低复杂度初始化；对量子寄存器宽度、门计数和查询复杂度进行分析，并在Qiskit中进行理想与有噪声的量子电路仿真。

Result: 仿真表明在理想量子环境下能接近ML性能并实现Grover平方加速；在噪声环境下，低深度电路与MMSE初始化使退相干影响可忽略，读出误差引入中等降级但仍接近MMSE性能；算法对信道长度和RIS规模表现出鲁棒性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该论文证明了将最大似然检测重构为QUBO并用GAS求解，在理想量子条件下可实现接近ML性能并保持Grover平方加速；在有噪声情况下，通过低深度电路与MMSE初始化能缓解退相干影响，读出误差是主要性能下降来源，但整体仍接近MMSE基线，表明方法在RIS辅助宽带通信中可行。

Abstract: Wideband and low-latency requirements in sixth-generation (6G) networks
demand detectors that approach maximum-likelihood (ML) performance without
incurring exponential complexity. This work develops a hybrid quantum-classical
detection framework for reconfigurable intelligent surface (RIS)-assisted
single-carrier (SC) frequency-domain equalization (FDE) over
frequency-selective channels. The ML detection objective is reformulated as a
quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) problem and solved via
Grover adaptive search (GAS). To accelerate convergence, we introduce a
frequency-domain MMSE threshold that exploits the circulant structure of SC-FDE
channels, yielding low-complexity initialization. The framework is evaluated
across varying channel lengths and RIS sizes, confirming robustness and
scalability. In addition, GAS requirements are quantified through register
widths and gate counts, and its query complexity is analyzed to characterize
the algorithm's cost for block transmission in frequency-selective channels.
Quantum circuit simulations are conducted in Qiskit under both ideal and noisy
conditions. In the ideal case, the detector achieves near-optimal performance
while benefiting from Grover's quadratic speedup, reducing the search cost from
from O(M^N) exhaustive evaluations to O(SQRT(M^N)) oracle queries. Under noise,
the shallow depth of the GAS circuits, aided by MMSE initialization, makes
depolarizing errors negligible, while readout errors introduce moderate
degradation yet still preserve performance close to the MMSE baseline. These
results establish the feasibility of quantum-enhanced detection for
RIS-assisted broadband communications, highlighting both algorithmic
scalability and practical robustness for 6G networks.

</details>


### [2] [Improving dynamic congestion isolation in data-center networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04639)
*Alberto Merino,Jesus Escudero-Sahuquillo,Pedro Javier Garcia,Francisco J. Quiles*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: ICI是一种将拥塞隔离信息用于指导DCQCN/ECN标记的协同机制，从而减少误报与不必要的速率抑制，显著降低BECN数量并改善尾延迟，同时保持吞吐与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代分布式AI和大规模应用引起的数据中心网络频繁出现incast及网络内部拥塞，现有注入限速（如DCQCN）慢、或拥塞隔离需交换机额外逻辑，单独使用各有不足，联合使用又会导致误判和资源低效，因此需要一种更高效的协同机制。

Method: 提出一种名为ICI的机制：在CI已隔离拥塞流的基础上，将该信息反馈给运行DCQCN的端节点/ECN标记逻辑，使得交换机在标记ECN时排除受害流，避免触发错误的闭环减速；并优化标记策略以更快响应微突发。

Result: 在多种流量模式（包含incast与典型数据中心负载）评估中，ICI将生成的BECN数量最多降低32倍，尾延迟最多提升31%，同时保持高吞吐与可扩展性。

Conclusion: ICI通过协同CI与DCQCN，避免将受害流误判为拥塞流，从而减少错误ECN标记和不必要的速率抑制，提高响应性与延迟表现。

Abstract: The rise of distributed AI and large-scale applications has impacted the
communication operations of data-center and Supercomputer interconnection
networks, leading to dramatic incast or in-network congestion scenarios and
challenging existing congestion control mechanisms, such as injection
throttling (e.g., DCQCN) or congestion isolation (CI). While DCQCN provides a
scalable traffic rate adjustment for congesting flows at end nodes (which is
slow) and CI effectively isolates these flows in special network resources
(which requires extra logic in the switches), their combined use, although it
diminishes their particular drawbacks, leads to false congestion scenarios
identification and signaling, excessive throttling, and inefficient network
resource utilization. In this paper, we propose a new CI mechanism, called
Improved Congestion Isolation (ICI), which efficiently combines CI and DCQCN so
that the information of the isolated congesting flows is used to guide the ECN
marking performed by DCQCN in a way that victim flows do not end up being
marked. This coordination reduces false-positive congestion detection,
suppresses unnecessary closed-loop feedback (i.e., wrong congestion
notifications), and improves responsiveness to communication microbursts.
Evaluated under diverse traffic patterns, including incast and Data-center
workloads, ICI reduces the number of generated BECNs by up to 32x and improves
tail latency by up to 31%, while maintaining high throughput and scalability.

</details>

### [3] [OMPILOT: Harnessing Transformer Models for Auto Parallelization to Shared Memory Computing Paradigms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03866)
*Arijit Bhattacharjee,Ali TehraniJamsaz,Le Chen,Niranjan Hasabnis,Mihai Capota,Nesreen Ahmed,Ali Jannesari*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出专门用于将C++转为OpenMP的编码器-解码器Transformer（OMPILOT），通过并行语义预训练与函数级建模提升翻译质量，并引入OMPBLEU来评估OpenMP生成的正确性与质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM与传统规则系统相比在代码翻译上更灵活，但现有工作侧重于循环级转换，缺乏函数级上下文与并行语义特定的训练目标，导致生成OpenMP指令时易出错。

Method: 结合无监督和有监督学习：自定义预训练目标融入并行构造语义（如同步、共享/私有变量、循环并行化模式）、在函数级别进行编码解码以捕捉更广语境，并使用并行化语义增强的数据增强与微调策略。

Result: 提出OMPILOT模型和OMPBLEU评估指标，声称比以往工作在OpenMP构造正确性和质量上更优（文中应有实验验证，但摘要未给出具体数值）。

Conclusion: OMPILOT提出了一种针对C++到OpenMP并行化的专用编码器-解码器Transformer，旨在在函数级别捕捉更广泛的语义并通过自定义预训练目标融合并行构造语义，从而提高代码翻译的健壮性。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have significantly
accelerated progress in code translation, enabling more accurate and efficient
transformation across programming languages. While originally developed for
natural language processing, LLMs have shown strong capabilities in modeling
programming language syntax and semantics, outperforming traditional rule-based
systems in both accuracy and flexibility. These models have streamlined
cross-language conversion, reduced development overhead, and accelerated legacy
code migration. In this paper, we introduce OMPILOT, a novel domain-specific
encoder-decoder transformer tailored for translating C++ code into OpenMP,
enabling effective shared-memory parallelization. OMPILOT leverages custom
pre-training objectives that incorporate the semantics of parallel constructs
and combines both unsupervised and supervised learning strategies to improve
code translation robustness. Unlike previous work that focused primarily on
loop-level transformations, OMPILOT operates at the function level to capture a
wider semantic context. To evaluate our approach, we propose OMPBLEU, a novel
composite metric specifically crafted to assess the correctness and quality of
OpenMP parallel constructs, addressing limitations in conventional translation
metrics.

</details>


### [4] [Stochastic Modeling for Energy-Efficient Edge Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03941)
*Fabio Diniz Rossi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Markov chain modeling and Monte Carlo validation show AI-driven predictive power scaling lowers energy use and improves responsiveness for heterogeneous edge nodes by anticipating workloads and optimizing state transitions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Edge devices have limited energy and distributed management; predicting workload to proactively scale power states can reduce transitions and energy waste compared to reactive methods.

Method: Use discrete-time Markov chains to model power state transitions; derive steady-state probabilities and expected energy consumption; validate via Monte Carlo simulations; perform sensitivity analysis on transition probabilities.

Result: Theoretical and simulation results align closely; predictive scaling reduces transitions, energy consumption disparities among nodes, and improves adaptive coordination in multi-node setups.

Conclusion: AI-based predictive power management significantly improves energy efficiency and responsiveness in edge computing by minimizing unnecessary power state transitions and balancing workload across heterogeneous nodes.

Abstract: Edge Computing enables low-latency processing for real-time applications but
introduces challenges in power management due to the distributed nature of edge
devices and their limited energy resources. This paper proposes a stochastic
modeling approach using Markov Chains to analyze power state transitions in
Edge Computing. By deriving steady-state probabilities and evaluating energy
consumption, we demonstrate the benefits of AI-driven predictive power scaling
over conventional reactive methods. Monte Carlo simulations validate the model,
showing strong alignment between theoretical and empirical results. Sensitivity
analysis highlights how varying transition probabilities affect power
efficiency, confirming that predictive scaling minimizes unnecessary
transitions and improves overall system responsiveness. Our findings suggest
that AI-based power management strategies significantly enhance energy
efficiency by anticipating workload demands and optimizing state transitions.
Experimental results indicate that AI-based power management optimizes workload
distribution across heterogeneous edge nodes, reducing energy consumption
disparities between devices, improving overall efficiency, and enhancing
adaptive power coordination in multi-node environments.

</details>


### [5] [Parallel Spawning Strategies for Dynamic-Aware MPI Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04268)
*Iker Martín-Álvarez,José I. Aliaga,Maribel Castillo,Sergio Iserte*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出协作并行spawn策略，既避免重启代价又能快速释放节点，扩展开销小，收缩加速显著，适用于共享与异构环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MPI可塑性方法要么重启整个应用代价高昂，要么在收缩时无法完全释放节点资源，影响系统利用率与等待时间，需降低重配置成本。

Method: 设计并实现了一个并行spawn算法，使所有进程在扩展时协同创建新进程并在收缩时正确释放跨节点的进程，支持异构与共享资源环境。

Result: 在同构与异构系统上验证，扩展时间仅增加最多1.25×的开销，而收缩操作成本至少降低20×，显著缩短调度使得系统makespan降低。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种新颖的并行生成策略，通过在重新分配前让所有进程协作生成，从而减少重构时间并解决MPI可伸缩性收缩时未能释放资源的问题。

Abstract: Dynamic resource management is an increasingly important capability of High
Performance Computing systems, as it enables jobs to adjust their resource
allocation at runtime. This capability has been shown to reduce workload
makespan, substantially decrease job waiting times and improve overall system
utilization. In this context, malleability refers to the ability of
applications to adapt to new resource allocations during execution. Although
beneficial, malleability incurs significant reconfiguration costs, making the
reduction of these costs an important research topic.
  Some existing methods for MPI applications respawn the entire application,
which is an expensive solution that avoids the reuse of original processes.
Other MPI methods reuse them, but fail to fully release unneeded processes when
shrinking, since some ranks within the same communicator remain active across
nodes, preventing the application from returning those nodes to the system.
This work overcomes both limitations by proposing a novel parallel spawning
strategy, in which all processes cooperate in spawning before redistribution,
thereby reducing execution time. Additionally, it removes shrinkage
limitations, allowing better adaptation of parallel systems to workload and
reducing their makespan. As a result, it preserves competitive expansion times
with at most a $1.25\times$ overhead, while enabling fast shrink operations
that reduce their cost by at least $20\times$. This strategy has been validated
on both homogeneous and heterogeneous systems and can also be applied in
shared-resource environments.

</details>


### [6] [Enabling Dynamic Sparsity in Quantized LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04477)
*Rongxiang Wang,Kangyuan Shu,Felix Xiaozhu Lin*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出一种使动态激活稀疏性与低比特分组量化协同的方案：之字形量化布局+专用GEMV内核+紧凑索引收集。实验证明在商用GPU上可在不损失精度下最多提升1.55x解码速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机是移动与桌面端部署LLM受限于内存与计算资源，尽管内部激活在输入上呈动态稀疏，但现有主流的分组量化与稀疏性难以兼容，限制了在终端设备上高效运行大模型的能力。

Method: 方法包括三部分：1) 之字形(zigzag)量化布局，将权重按与激活稀疏性一致的方式组织以提升GPU内存局部性；2) 针对该布局设计专用矩向量乘(GEMV)内核，充分利用并行计算单元；3) 轻量运行时机制，用于低开销地收集稀疏索引并触发相应计算。

Result: 在多个模型尺度和硬件配置上，该方案在保持与密集量化推理相当的精度前提下，实现了最高1.55倍的解码吞吐量提升，证明了结构化稀疏性与量化可在商用GPU上共存。

Conclusion: 本文结论是：在低比特量化下，通过特定权重布局、定制GEMV内核和高效索引收集机制，可以在商用GPU上实现动态稀疏推理，从而在不损失精度的情况下显著提高解码吞吐量（最高1.55x）。

Abstract: Deploying large language models (LLMs) on end-user devices is gaining
importance due to benefits in responsiveness, privacy, and operational cost.
Yet the limited memory and compute capability of mobile and desktop GPUs make
efficient execution difficult. Recent observations suggest that the internal
activations of LLMs are often dynamically sparse, meaning that for each input,
only part of the network contributes significantly to the output. Such sparsity
could reduce computation, but it interacts poorly with group-wise quantization,
which remains the dominant approach for fitting LLMs onto resource-constrained
hardware. To reconcile these two properties, this study proposes a set of
techniques that realize dynamic sparse inference under low-bit quantization.
The method features: (1) a zigzag-patterned quantization layout that organizes
weights in a way consistent with activation sparsity and improves GPU memory
locality; (2) a specialized GEMV kernel designed for this layout to fully
utilize parallel compute units; and (3) a compact runtime mechanism that
gathers sparse indices with minimal overhead. Across several model scales and
hardware configurations, the approach achieves up to 1.55x faster decoding
throughput while maintaining accuracy comparable to dense quantized inference,
showing that structured sparsity and quantization can effectively coexist on
commodity GPUs.

</details>


### [7] [A New Probabilistic Mobile Byzantine Failure Model for Self-Protecting Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04523)
*Silvia Bonomi,Giovanni Farina,Roy Friedman,Eviatar B. Procaccia,Sebastien Tixeuil*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出一个概率移动拜占庭失败模型，嵌入MAPE-K Analysis，数学分析感染与恢复速率对系统安全状态转换时间的影响，并用仿真验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固定拜占庭模型无法准确反映现实中随时间演化的攻击行为，需在系统设计阶段引入可捕捉动态攻击的概率模型以增强自我保护能力。

Method: 基于MAPE-K架构，将新的概率MBF模型嵌入Analysis模块；对拜占庭感染传播与自愈过程建立随机过程/马尔可夫模型，推导到达特定拜占庭节点阈值及恢复时间的数学公式；并用仿真验证理论结果。

Result: 推导了在不同感染与恢复速率下，系统达到不安全阈值或自愈成功的时间分布；仿真结果与理论分析一致，展示了模型用于驱动自我保护重配置策略的可行性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一个可插拔的概率移动拜占庭失败（MBF）模型，用于MAPE-K架构的Analysis组件，以捕捉攻击动态并驱动自我保护与重配置策略。数学分析与仿真表明，在感染传播率与自愈率影响下，系统会在阈值时间内进入不安全状态或恢复到安全状态。

Abstract: Modern distributed systems face growing security threats, as attackers
continuously enhance their skills and vulnerabilities span across the entire
system stack, from hardware to the application layer. In the system design
phase, fault tolerance techniques can be employed to safeguard systems. From a
theoretical perspective, an attacker attempting to compromise a system can be
abstracted by considering the presence of Byzantine processes in the system.
Although this approach enhances the resilience of the distributed system, it
introduces certain limitations regarding the accuracy of the model in
reflecting real-world scenarios. In this paper, we consider a self-protecting
distributed system based on the \emph{Monitoring-Analyse-Plan-Execute over a
shared Knowledge} (MAPE-K) architecture, and we propose a new probabilistic
Mobile Byzantine Failure (MBF) that can be plugged into the Analysis component.
Our new model captures the dynamics of evolving attacks and can be used to
drive the self-protection and reconfiguration strategy. We analyze
mathematically the time that it takes until the number of Byzantine nodes
crosses given thresholds, or for the system to self-recover back into a safe
state, depending on the rates of Byzantine infection spreading \emph{vs.} the
rate of self-recovery. We also provide simulation results that illustrate the
behavior of the system under such assumptions.

</details>


### [8] [Resolving Conflicts with Grace: Dynamically Concurrent Universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04631)
*Petr Kuznetsov,Nathan Josia Schrodt*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出动态并发概念和一个对应的通用构造，使操作仅在实际冲突时才使用强同步，旨在提高分布式系统的并发性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同步是分布式计算可扩展性的主要障碍；许多并发操作仅在罕见状态下冲突，因此希望能动态检测冲突并仅在必要时进行同步以减少开销。

Method: 作者定义了"动态并发"概念：根据当前系统状态，操作仅在必须与并发操作仲裁时才使用强同步原语。基于此概念，构建了一个动态并发的通用构造（universal construction），可能结合冲突检测机制和条件使用强同步的策略来执行操作。

Result: 提出的动态并发通用构造能够根据系统状态自适应使用同步，从而减少不必要的同步，提升并发性和可扩展性（在摘要中未给出具体性能数据）。

Conclusion: 本文提出并实现了一个动态并发的通用构造，允许操作仅在实际发生冲突时使用强同步，从而提高分布式系统的可扩展性。

Abstract: Synchronization is the major obstacle to scalability in distributed
computing. Concurrent operations on the shared data engage in synchronization
when they encounter a \emph{conflict}, i.e., their effects depend on the order
in which they are applied. Ideally, one would like to detect conflicts in a
\emph{dynamic} manner, i.e., adjusting to the current system state. Indeed, it
is very common that two concurrent operations conflict only in some rarely
occurring states. In this paper, we define the notion of \emph{dynamic
concurrency}: an operation employs strong synchronization primitives only if it
\emph{has} to arbitrate with concurrent operations, given the current system
state. We then present a dynamically concurrent universal construction.

</details>

### [9] [Temporal Analysis Framework for Intrusion Detection Systems: A Novel Taxonomy for Time-Aware Cybersecurity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03799)
*Tatiana S. Parlanti,Carlos A. Catania*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文通过系统综述提出了一个按时间处理能力对NIDS方法进行分类的框架，指出跨流序列与时间窗口方法有利于早期检测，并警示数据集存在的晚期攻击偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前入侵检测多集中在攻击后期指征，导致发现滞后，亟需时间感知方法以实现前瞻性防御。

Method: 系统综述了2020-2025年40余篇研究，依据对时间的处理（静态单流、流内时间特征、多窗口、跨流序列建模）对NIDS方法进行分类并构建时序覆盖矩阵与与ATT&CK战术映射。

Result: 发现跨流序列与时间窗口方法在覆盖MITRE ATT&CK战术上最全面；并揭示主流数据集偏向晚期攻击，阻碍早期检测研究。

Conclusion: 提出的时序分析框架与分类法表明，跨流序列和时间窗口方法能够覆盖更广的攻击阶段，从侦察到影响，从而支持更早期的检测。

Abstract: Most intrusion detection systems still identify attacks only after
significant damage has occurred, detecting late-stage tactics rather than early
indicators of compromise. This paper introduces a temporal analysis framework
and taxonomy for time-aware network intrusion detection. Through a systematic
review of over 40 studies published between 2020 and 2025, we classify NIDS
methods according to their treatment of time, from static per-flow analysis to
multi-window sequential modeling. The proposed taxonomy reveals that inter-flow
sequential and temporal window-based methods provide the broadest temporal
coverage across MITRE ATT&CK tactics, enabling detection from Reconnaissance
through Impact stages. Our analysis further exposes systematic bias in widely
used datasets, which emphasize late-stage attacks and thus limit progress
toward early detection. This framework provides essential groundwork for
developing IDS capable of anticipating rather than merely reacting to cyber
threats, advancing the field toward truly proactive defense mechanisms.

</details>


### [10] [OTS-PC: OTS-based Payment Channels for the Lightning Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04021)
*Sergio Demian Lerner,Ariel Autoransky*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 用一次性签名和状态序列号实现更简洁、高效且兼容Lightning的双向支付通道，具备O(1)存储和更低信息泄露。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低现有双向支付通道（如Poon-Dryja/Lightning）的复杂性与状态存储开销，同时减少信息泄露并保持与现有路由机制的兼容性。

Method: 使用一次性签名(one-time signatures)结合状态序列号来构造通道更新机制，避免依赖复杂的惩罚交易序列，通道维护采用O(1)存储策略，设计兼容Lightning Network路由方案。

Result: 构造实现了每个通道常数级别的存储需求、最小化状态泄露，并保持与Lightning路由兼容；论文宣称整体更简单且具若干实用优点。

Conclusion: 提出了一种基于一次性签名和状态序列号的新型双向支付通道，相较于Poon-Dryja构造更简单，并在存储、信息泄露与路由兼容性上有优势。

Abstract: We present a new type of bidirectional payment channel based on One-Time
Signatures on state sequence numbers. This new construction is simpler than the
Poon-Dryja construction, but provides a number of benefits such as $O(1)$
storage per channel, minimal information leakage, and compatibility with
Lightning Network routing.

of spreading child sexual abuse material on the clear web. The campaign
utilized at least 1,026 web pages for at least 738,286 registered users. Our
analysis details the operation of such a campaign, showcasing how social

### [12] [Security Analysis of Agentic AI Communication Protocols: A Comparative Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03841)
*Yedidel Louck,Ariel Stulman,Amit Dvir*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 对CORAL、ACP和A2A进行14点漏洞基准测试：CORAL架构强但实现有致命认证授权漏洞；ACP可选完整性机制导致高危完整性和机密性问题；建议两者结合的混合设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI驱动的多智能体系统在复杂分布式工作流中的广泛应用，其通信协议安全性尚未得到充分研究与比较，需要实证分析现有协议的弱点以指导更安全的设计。

Method: 通过构建14点漏洞分类法（认证、授权、完整性、机密性、可用性等维度），对官方CORAL实现、SDK实现的ACP以及基于文献的A2A评估进行系统测试与比较，包括动态测试、代码审计与协议模糊测试。

Result: 发现CORAL在传输层消息校验与会话隔离上架构坚实，但在SSE网关处存在认证与授权失效的实现漏洞。ACP的灵活性（如可选JWS）导致可被绕过的完整性与机密性缺陷。总体上，现有协议普遍不足。

Conclusion: 本文结论表明，尽管CORAL在架构层面表现稳健，但其实现存在严重认证与授权缺陷；ACP则因可选的每消息完整性机制导致高风险的完整性与机密性问题。建议采用结合CORAL架构与ACP强制性每消息完整性保障的混合方案。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) powered by artificial intelligence (AI) are
increasingly foundational to complex, distributed workflows. Yet, the security
of their underlying communication protocols remains critically under-examined.
This paper presents the first empirical, comparative security analysis of the
official CORAL implementation and a high-fidelity, SDK-based ACP
implementation, benchmarked against a literature-based evaluation of A2A. Using
a 14 point vulnerability taxonomy, we systematically assess their defenses
across authentication, authorization, integrity, confidentiality, and
availability. Our results reveal a pronounced security dichotomy: CORAL
exhibits a robust architectural design, particularly in its transport-layer
message validation and session isolation, but suffers from critical
implementation-level vulnerabilities, including authentication and
authorization failures at its SSE gateway. Conversely, ACP's architectural
flexibility, most notably its optional JWS enforcement, translates into
high-impact integrity and confidentiality flaws. We contextualize these
findings within current industry trends, highlighting that existing protocols
remain insufficiently secure. As a path forward, we recommend a hybrid approach
that combines CORAL's integrated architecture with ACP's mandatory per-message
integrity guarantees, laying the groundwork for resilient, next-generation
agent communications.

### [13] [Secure Code Generation at Scale with Reflexion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03898)
*Arup Datta,Ahmed Aljohani,Hyunsook Do*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: LLMs生成代码常含安全缺陷（约1/4），反思式多轮提示能在1-2轮内显著减少不安全代码，尤其对模板化漏洞效果好，对弱加密/配置类问题效果较差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLMs广泛用于代码生成与重构，但生成的工作代码并不保证安全，需量化并改进LLM生成代码的安全性。

Method: 使用Instruct Prime数据集消除合规提示和线索污染；评估五种指令微调的代码LLM，比较零次基线和三轮反思提示；使用Insecure Code Detector (ICD) 自动检测安全问题；按照语言和CWE家族计算Repair、Regression、NetGain等指标。

Result: 零次提示下25-33%程序不安全，弱密码学与配置相关漏洞最难避免，模板化漏洞（XSS、代码注入、硬编码密钥）相对更易处理；Python安全率最高，C和C#最低；反思提示在第一轮带来最大提升，总体平均准确率提升近9个百分点；一到两轮反思足以带来大部分收益。

Conclusion: LLMs普遍能生成可运行代码但安全性仍不足，初始零次提示约25-33%程序存在安全缺陷；通过反思(reflexion)提示能显著提升安全性，主要在前1-2轮实现大部分改进，平均准确率从70.74%提升至79.43%。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now widely used to draft and refactor code,
but code that works is not necessarily secure. We evaluate secure code
generation using the Instruct Prime, which eliminated compliance-required
prompts and cue contamination, and evaluate five instruction-tuned code LLMs
using a zero-shot baseline and a three-round reflexion prompting approach.
Security is measured using the Insecure Code Detector (ICD), and results are
reported by measuring Repair, Regression, and NetGain metrics, considering the
programming language and CWE family. Our findings show that insecurity remains
common at the first round: roughly 25-33% of programs are insecure at a
zero-shot baseline (t0 ). Weak cryptography/config-dependent bugs are the
hardest to avoid while templated ones like XSS, code injection, and hard-coded
secrets are handled more reliably. Python yields the highest secure rates; C
and C# are the lowest, with Java, JS, PHP, and C++ in the middle. Reflexion
prompting improves security for all models, improving average accuracy from
70.74% at t0 to 79.43% at t3 , with the largest gains in the first round
followed by diminishing returns. The trends with Repair, Regression, and
NetGain metrics show that applying one to two rounds produces most of the
benefits. A replication package is available at
https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.17065846.

### [14] [Design and Detection of Covert Man-in-the-Middle Cyberattacks on Water Treatment Plants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03971)

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了利用系统辨识设计隐蔽MitM控制器的建模评估框架，并通过水处理类二阶含时延模型的仿真表明：噪声与模型不精确性显著影响攻击隐蔽性，现有PASAD检测在非理想条件下可部分识别此类攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对关键基础设施（如水处理厂）面临的隐蔽化MitM攻击威胁，研究攻击者如何利用系统辨识技术获得工艺动态模型并据此设计隐蔽控制策略，从而量化攻击的隐蔽性与现有检测方法的有效性，以推动更鲁棒的检测方案。

Method: 基于二阶线性时不变含时延模型建立被控过程，攻击者通过系统辨识得到被控系统模型并设计隐蔽控制器（Covert Controller）实施中间人攻击；防御方采用PASAD（Process-Aware Stealthy Attack Detection）检测算法评估攻击的可检测性；在不同噪声水平和攻击者模型不精确条件下进行数值仿真比较检测指标。

Result: 仿真结果显示：1) 在理想（低噪声、精确模型）条件下，攻击可高度隐蔽且难以被PASAD检测；2) 随噪声增大或攻击者模型误差增大，攻击残差与检测统计量变大，检测率提高；3) 存在阈值效应——超过一定模型误差或噪声水平，隐蔽攻击变得可被检测，从而提示需要改进检测器或结合多种检测机制。

Conclusion: 该论文表明，通过系统辨识获取模型并部署隐蔽控制器，攻击者可以在存在噪声和模型不精确性的情况下对水处理类连续过程实施难以检测的中间人攻击，但检测性能会随噪声增大和模型误差增大而下降。

Abstract: Cyberattacks targeting critical infrastructures, such as water treatment
facilities, represent significant threats to public health, safety, and the
environment. This paper introduces a systematic approach for modeling and
assessing covert man-in-the-middle (MitM) attacks that leverage system
identification techniques to inform the attack design. We focus on the
attacker's ability to deploy a covert controller, and we evaluate
countermeasures based on the Process-Aware Stealthy Attack Detection (PASAD)
anomaly detection method. Using a second-order linear time-invariant with time
delay model, representative of water treatment dynamics, we design and simulate
stealthy attacks. Our results highlight how factors such as system noise and
inaccuracies in the attacker's plant model influence the attack's stealthiness,
underscoring the need for more robust detection strategies in industrial
control environments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Software fuzzing has become a cornerstone in automated vulnerability
discovery, yet existing mutation strategies often lack semantic awareness,
leading to redundant test cases and slow exploration of deep program states. In
this work, I present a hybrid fuzzing framework that integrates static and
dynamic analysis with Large Language Model (LLM)-guided input mutation and
semantic feedback. Static analysis extracts control-flow and data-flow
information, which is transformed into structured prompts for the LLM to
generate syntactically valid and semantically diverse inputs. During execution,
I augment traditional coverage-based feedback with semantic feedback
signals-derived from program state changes, exception types, and output
semantics-allowing the fuzzer to prioritize inputs that trigger novel program
behaviors beyond mere code coverage. I implement our approach atop AFL++,
combining program instrumentation with embedding-based semantic similarity
metrics to guide seed selection. Evaluation on real-world open-source targets,
including libpng, tcpdump, and sqlite, demonstrates that our method achieves
faster time-to-first-bug, higher semantic diversity, and a competitive number
of unique bugs compared to state-of-the-art fuzzers. This work highlights the

combining TPOT's automated pipeline selection with SHAP interpretability, this
approach improves the accuracy and transparency of DDoS detection. Experimental

minimum forward packet header length are critical in detecting DDoS attacks,
offering a scalable and explainable cybersecurity solution.

### [17] [Black-Box Guardrail Reverse-engineering Attack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04215)
*Hongwei Yao,Yun Xia,Shuo Shao,Haoran Shi,Tong Qiao,Cong Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 作者提出一种基于强化学习和遗传算法的数据增强方法（GRA）来黑盒逆向工程LLM守护。实验证明在低成本下可高精度提取守护规则，揭示了显著的安全隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM部署越来越多地依赖守护以限制不当输出，这些守护的可观察决策模式本身成为攻击目标。作者旨在评估黑盒场景下能否从输入-输出对中重建守护策略，从而量化相关风险。

Method: 提出GRA（Guardrail Reverse-engineering Attack），基于强化学习框架，结合遗传算法驱动的数据增强（变异与交叉）来生成候选输入，优先采集与受害守护输出差异较大的样本，迭代构建高保真替代模型。

Result: 在ChatGPT、DeepSeek、Qwen3三大商业系统上实验，GRA在API费用低于85美元的情况下，规则匹配率超过0.92，说明该攻击在现实系统上高效可行。

Conclusion: 该工作首次提出了黑盒环境下对LLM安全守护（guardrail）进行反向工程的可行性和方法，证明了通过交互式查询与进化策略可以在低成本下高精度复现守护策略，因而暴露了现有守护设计的重要安全风险。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly employ guardrails to enforce
ethical, legal, and application-specific constraints on their outputs. While
effective at mitigating harmful responses, these guardrails introduce a new
class of vulnerabilities by exposing observable decision patterns. In this
work, we present the first study of black-box LLM guardrail reverse-engineering
attacks. We propose Guardrail Reverse-engineering Attack (GRA), a reinforcement
learning-based framework that leverages genetic algorithm-driven data
augmentation to approximate the decision-making policy of victim guardrails. By
iteratively collecting input-output pairs, prioritizing divergence cases, and
applying targeted mutations and crossovers, our method incrementally converges
toward a high-fidelity surrogate of the victim guardrail. We evaluate GRA on
three widely deployed commercial systems, namely ChatGPT, DeepSeek, and Qwen3,
and demonstrate that it achieves an rule matching rate exceeding 0.92 while
requiring less than $85 in API costs. These findings underscore the practical
feasibility of guardrail extraction and highlight significant security risks
for current LLM safety mechanisms. Our findings expose critical vulnerabilities
in current guardrail designs and highlight the urgent need for more robust
defense mechanisms in LLM deployment.

### [18] [A Parallel Region-Adaptive Differential Privacy Framework for Image Pixelization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04261)
*Ming Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率视觉感知与基础模型广泛部署导致视频隐私风险增加，传统差分隐私像素化在保真度、可扩展性与实时部署方面存在不足。

Method: 基于区域复杂度估计对图像分区，每一区域自适应选择像素化网格与拉普拉斯噪声尺度；并行化实现使各区域在GPU上同时处理；仅保存必要的噪声统计量以降低存储。

Result: 在PETS、Venice-2、PPM-100上实验显示良好隐私-效用平衡以及显著的运行时和存储减少；在CelebA上的人脸重新识别攻击实验证明能有效防止身份推断。

Abstract: The widespread deployment of high-resolution visual sensing systems, coupled
with the rise of foundation models, has amplified privacy risks in video-based
applications. Differentially private pixelization offers mathematically
guaranteed protection for visual data through grid-based noise addition, but
challenges remain in preserving task-relevant fidelity, achieving scalability,
and enabling efficient real-time deployment. To address this, we propose a
novel parallel, region-adaptive pixelization framework that combines the
theoretical rigor of differential privacy with practical efficiency. Our method
adaptively adjusts grid sizes and noise scales based on regional complexity,
leveraging GPU parallelism to achieve significant runtime acceleration compared
to the classical baseline. A lightweight storage scheme is introduced by
retaining only essential noisy statistics, significantly reducing space
overhead. Formal privacy analysis is provided under the Laplace mechanism and
parallel composition theorem. Extensive experiments on the PETS, Venice-2, and
PPM-100 datasets demonstrate favorable privacy-utility trade-offs and
significant runtime/storage reductions. A face re-identification attack
experiment on CelebA further confirms the method's effectiveness in preventing
identity inference. This validates its suitability for real-time
privacy-critical applications such as elderly care, smart home monitoring,
driver behavior analysis, and crowd behavior monitoring.

### [19] [Data Certification Strategies for Blockchain-based Traceability Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04409)
*Giacomo Zonneveld,Giulia Rafaiani,Massimo Battaglioni,Marco Baldi*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 针对持续产生的大量生产数据，本文比较分析了多种利用离链缓冲与Merkle树等结构将认证元数据写入区块链的策略，强调在成本、实时性与可验证性间需要权衡选择合适方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单条数据的区块链认证较为简单，但对持续高频产生的大量数据，直接逐条写链不可行。需要研究如何在保证去中心化验证与可审计性的同时，最小化链上成本与保持适当实时性。

Method: 构建典型生产过程追溯系统模型，设计若干认证策略（例如周期性批量提交、按事件触发提交、分层Merkle树与滚动哈希等混合方案），并通过复杂性分析与实验比较其链上交易量、离链存储需求、证明大小与验证时间等指标。

Result: 提出的策略在不同场景下表现各有优劣：批量周期提交在链上成本低但实时性差；事件触发提交适合关键事件但开销不稳定；分层Merkle等混合方案在可扩展性与验证效率间取得平衡。实现上可通过温冷数据分层、证据压缩和可更新签名等手段进一步优化。

Conclusion: 本文提出并比较分析了多种将持续产生的大量生产数据通过离链缓冲区与Merkle树等结构组织后，写入区块链以实现可去中心化验证的认证策略。结论指出，针对不同应用需求（如实时性、存储与计算开销、可验证性）没有单一最优方案，应在吞吐、延迟、链上成本与审计灵活性之间权衡选择适合的策略。

Abstract: The use of blockchains for data certification and traceability is now well
established in both the literature and practical applications. However, while
blockchain-based certification of individual data is clear and straightforward,
the use of blockchain to certify large amounts of data produced on a nearly
continuous basis still poses some challenges. In such a case, in fact, it is
first necessary to collect the data in an off-chain buffer, and then to
organize it, e.g., via Merkle trees, in order to keep the size and quantity of
certification data to be written to the blockchain small. In this paper, we
consider a typical system for blockchain-based traceability of a production
process, and propose and comparatively analyze some strategies for certifying
the data of such a process on blockchain, while maintaining the possibility of
verifying their certification in a decentralized way.

</details>


### [20] [Adversarially Robust and Interpretable Magecart Malware Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04440)
*Pedro Pereira,José Gouveia,João Vitorino,Eva Maia,Isabel Praça*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 通过比较若干传统机器学习模型、引入行为DFA特征及对抗训练，该研究在真实数据上实现了对Magecart攻击的高效、可解释和鲁棒检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Magecart攻击对客户端安全和在线支付信任构成严重威胁，需要可解释且对抗鲁棒的检测方法。

Method: 比较了树模型、线性模型和核方法，进行了超参数调优与特征选择；使用行为确定性DFA从脚本执行日志提取结构行为特征；对模型进行对抗训练并使用Adversarial Robustness Toolbox和Adaptative Perturbation Pattern Method进行对抗评估；提供了简洁的决策解释。

Result: 实验在真实数据集上显示了高检测性能和可解释的决策，证明了所提方法在实际网页安全场景中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文表明传统机器学习模型在检测Magecart注入攻击方面有效，且结合行为DFA和可解释性方法能提高鲁棒性与透明性。

Abstract: Magecart skimming attacks have emerged as a significant threat to client-side
security and user trust in online payment systems. This paper addresses the
challenge of achieving robust and explainable detection of Magecart attacks
through a comparative study of various Machine Learning (ML) models with a
real-world dataset. Tree-based, linear, and kernel-based models were applied,
further enhanced through hyperparameter tuning and feature selection, to
distinguish between benign and malicious scripts. Such models are supported by
a Behavior Deterministic Finite Automaton (DFA) which captures structural
behavior patterns in scripts, helping to analyze and classify client-side
script execution logs. To ensure robustness against adversarial evasion
attacks, the ML models were adversarially trained and evaluated using attacks
from the Adversarial Robustness Toolbox and the Adaptative Perturbation Pattern
Method. In addition, concise explanations of ML model decisions are provided,
supporting transparency and user trust. Experimental validation demonstrated
high detection performance and interpretable reasoning, demonstrating that
traditional ML models can be effective in real-world web security contexts.

</details>


### [21] [Exploiting Data Structures for Bypassing and Crashing Anti-Malware Solutions via Telemetry Complexity Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04472)
*Evgenios Gkritsis,Constantinos Patsakis,George Stergiopoulos*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文发现并实证化“遥测复杂性攻击”，即通过生成深度/超大遥测数据击溃分析与存储管道，使恶意行为未被记录或呈现；对十二款产品测试表明七款受影响，提出修复建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反恶意软件系统依赖复杂的遥测管道（采集代理、序列化、数据库、可视化等），这些组件本应处理大量行为数据，但其处理能力往往是有界的。作者发现攻击者无需绕过传感器或提权，仅需通过制造异常遥测负载即可使处理链路失效，从而使检测与分析失效。

Method: 作者通过递归生成大量子进程，产生特制的、深度嵌套且超大尺寸的遥测数据，触发序列化、存储和可视化层面的边界限制（如 JSON/BSON 的深度与大小限制），测试了十二款商用与开源的恶意软件分析平台和 EDR 解决方案，记录失败点并获得若干产品的修复与 CVE 编号。

Result: 在被测试的十二款产品中，七款在遥测管道的不同阶段出现失败（如报告被截断、数据库插入被拒绝、序列化递归/大小错误、仪表盘无响应等）；两家厂商获得 CVE-2025-61301 与 CVE-2025-61303，其他厂商则通过补丁或配置调整缓解了问题。作者还分析了根本原因并提出了多项缓解建议以防范 DoA 攻击。

Conclusion: 本文提出并验证了一类新型漏洞——遥测复杂性攻击（Telemetry Complexity Attacks, TCAs），通过滥用数据采集与处理系统的容量与深度限制，导致反恶意软件产品产生“分析拒绝（Denial-of-Analysis, DoA）”状态，从而使恶意行为被执行但未被记录或展示。

Abstract: Anti-malware systems rely on sandboxes, hooks, and telemetry pipelines,
including collection agents, serializers, and database backends, to monitor
program and system behavior. We show that these data-handling components
constitute an exploitable attack surface that can lead to denial-of-analysis
(DoA) states without disabling sensors or requiring elevated privileges. As a
result, we present \textit{Telemetry Complexity Attacks} (TCAs), a new class of
vulnerabilities that exploit fundamental mismatches between unbounded
collection mechanisms and bounded processing capabilities. Our method
recursively spawns child processes to generate specially crafted, deeply
nested, and oversized telemetry that stresses serialization and storage
boundaries, as well as visualization layers, for example, JSON/BSON depth and
size limits. Depending on the product, this leads to truncated or missing
behavioral reports, rejected database inserts, serializer recursion and size
errors, and unresponsive dashboards. In all of these cases, malicious activity
is normally executed; however, depending on the examined solution, it is not
recorded and/or not presented to the analysts. Therefore, instead of evading
sensors, we break the pipeline that stores the data captured by the sensors.
  We evaluate our technique against twelve commercial and open-source malware
analysis platforms and endpoint detection and response (EDR) solutions. Seven
products fail in different stages of the telemetry pipeline; two vendors
assigned CVE identifiers (CVE-2025-61301 and CVE-2025-61303), and others issued
patches or configuration changes. We discuss root causes and propose mitigation
strategies to prevent DoA attacks triggered by adversarial telemetry.

</details>


### [22] [Large Language Models for Cyber Security](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04508)
*Raunak Somani,Aswani Kumar Cherukuri*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文主张将LLM引入网络安全，提出加密提示与四层集成架构，展示了LLM在提高检测准确性、可扩展性与抵抗提示注入方面的优越性，并推荐在IDS中采用解耦集成方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于规则和特征签名的安全系统难以应对利用AI的高级、动态化攻击，因而需要引入更具语境感知和自适应能力的智能模型来提升防御效果。

Method: 论文通过分析LLM的体系结构与工作原理，提出加密提示机制防范提示注入，并设计了一个四层架构用于将LLM整合进网络安全工具；对比了多种将LLM集成进传统IDS的方法并评估其性能，最终推荐解耦模型。

Result: 主要结果包括：加密提示与LLM结合能有效减轻提示注入攻击；LLM增强的安全工具在准确性、可扩展性与对新威胁的适应性上优于传统模型；解耦集成模型在IDS场景下表现最好。

Conclusion: 该论文结论认为将大语言模型（LLM）集成到网络安全工具与协议中，可提升检测与响应能力，特别是通过加密提示（Encrypted Prompt）可缓解提示注入攻击；LLM增强的系统在准确性、可扩展性与适应性方面优于传统模型；在入侵检测系统（IDS）中采用解耦模型是最优的集成方式。

Abstract: This paper studies the integration off Large Language Models into
cybersecurity tools and protocols. The main issue discussed in this paper is
how traditional rule-based and signature based security systems are not enough
to deal with modern AI powered cyber threats. Cybersecurity industry is
changing as threats are becoming more dangerous and adaptive in nature by
levering the features provided by AI tools. By integrating LLMs into these
tools and protocols, make the systems scalable, context-aware and intelligent.
Thus helping it to mitigate these evolving cyber threats. The paper studies the
architecture and functioning of LLMs, its integration into Encrypted prompts to
prevent prompt injection attacks. It also studies the integration of LLMs into
cybersecurity tools using a four layered architecture. At last, the paper has
tried to explain various ways of integration LLMs into traditional Intrusion
Detection System and enhancing its original abilities in various dimensions.
The key findings of this paper has been (i)Encrypted Prompt with LLM is an
effective way to mitigate prompt injection attacks, (ii) LLM enhanced cyber
security tools are more accurate, scalable and adaptable to new threats as
compared to traditional models, (iii) The decoupled model approach for LLM
integration into IDS is the best way as it is the most accurate way.

### [23] [Confidential Computing for Cloud Security: Exploring Hardware based Encryption Using Trusted Execution Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.04550)
*Dhruv Deepak Agarwal,Aswani Kumar Cherukuri*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文综述了Intel SGX与ARM TrustZone在机密计算中的架构与应用，认为TEEs对云中数据在用保护关键但面临安全、性能与部署挑战，需结合其他技术与改进才能广泛部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 云计算扩展了数据处理能力，但传统加密仅保护静态和传输中的数据，无法保护处理中的数据；因此需要研究硬件支持的TEEs以实现机密计算并提升云平台对敏感数据的安全保障。

Method: 通过详尽的文献综述，比较SGX与TrustZone的架构、隔离机制、密钥管理、证明与远程验证流程，以及现有部署与性能评估研究；分析实际应用案例与部署策略，并综合已知攻击/弱点评估其安全性。

Result: 文献综述显示TEEs能在很多场景下提供有效保护，支持远程证明与密钥封装来保证机密性与完整性；然而，性能开销、内存限制、侧信道风险、可信计算基减小问题、以及跨平台/跨租户的可扩展部署仍是主要障碍。建议结合软件隔离、形式化验证和专门的侧信道缓解措施，以及标准化API与云服务集成策略以提升实际可用性。

Conclusion: TEEs（如Intel SGX和ARM TrustZone）在保护云中数据处理阶段具有重要作用，能够显著减少数据在使用中被泄露的风险，但并非万能，仍存在侧信道攻击、可扩展性和集成复杂性等挑战。

Abstract: The growth of cloud computing has revolutionized data processing and storage
capacities to another levels of scalability and flexibility. But in the
process, it has created a huge challenge of security, especially in terms of
safeguarding sensitive data. Classical security practices, including encryption
at rest and during transit, fail to protect data in use and expose it to
various possible breaches. In response to this problem , Confidential Computing
has been a tool ,seeking to secure data in processing by usage of
hardware-based Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs). TEEs, including Intel's
Software Guard Extensions (SGX) and ARM's TrustZone, offers protected contexts
within the processor, where data is kept confidential ,intact and secure , even
with malicious software or compromised operating systems. In this research, we
have explored the architecture and security features of TEEs like Intel SGX and
ARM TrustZone, and their effectiveness in improving cloud data security. From a
thorough literature survey ,we have analyzed the deployment strategies,
performance indicators, and practical uses of these TEEs for the same purpose.
In addition, we have discussed the issues regarding deployment, possible
weaknesses, scalability issues, and integration issues. Our results focuses on
the central position of TEEs in strengthening and advancing cloud security
infrastructures, pointing towards their ability to create a secure foundation
for Confidential Computing.

</details>

### [24] [Applying Time Series Deep Learning Models to Forecast the Growth of Perennial Ryegrass in Ireland](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03749)
*Oluwadurotimi Onibonoje,Vuong M. Ngo,Andrew McCarre,Elodie Ruelle,Bernadette O-Briend,Mark Roantree*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 使用34年（1757周）单变量牧草高度数据训练的时序卷积网络可高精度预测多年牧草生长（RMSE2.74、MAE3.46），为爱尔兰奶业提供低成本、可靠的草产预测工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有牧草生长预测多依赖复杂且不切实际的机理模型，使用深度学习能提供更低成本、可扩展的预测方法，帮助提升爱尔兰奶业的盈利性与可持续性。

Method: 作者针对每周牧草高度的单变量时间序列，设计并训练了多种深度学习模型（以时序卷积网络为主），通过历史高度数据进行监督学习；使用长期（34年、1757周）数据集进行训练与验证，并进行了模型结构与超参数的系统探索以寻找最优配置。

Result: 提出的时序卷积网络在Cork地区多年数据上实现了RMSE=2.74和MAE=3.46的高性能；论文还报告了不同模型配置的对比与最佳实践，证明深度学习方法在单变量牧草预测任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文表明，针对单变量牧草生长数据，深度学习模型（尤其是时序卷积网络）能显著优于传统机制模型，且在爱尔兰多年长期数据上表现稳定，能够为奶业提供更可靠的产草预测，进而助力可持续农业实践。

Abstract: Grasslands, constituting the world's second-largest terrestrial carbon sink,
play a crucial role in biodiversity and the regulation of the carbon cycle.
Currently, the Irish dairy sector, a significant economic contributor, grapples
with challenges related to profitability and sustainability. Presently, grass
growth forecasting relies on impractical mechanistic models. In response, we
propose deep learning models tailored for univariate datasets, presenting
cost-effective alternatives. Notably, a temporal convolutional network designed
for forecasting Perennial Ryegrass growth in Cork exhibits high performance,
leveraging historical grass height data with RMSE of 2.74 and MAE of 3.46.
Validation across a comprehensive dataset spanning 1,757 weeks over 34 years
provides insights into optimal model configurations. This study enhances our
understanding of model behavior, thereby improving reliability in grass growth
forecasting and contributing to the advancement of sustainable dairy farming
practices.

### [25] [Federated Learning with Gramian Angular Fields for Privacy-Preserving ECG Classification on Heterogeneous IoT Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03753)
*Youssef Elmir,Yassine Himeur,Abbes Amira*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 将1D ECG转为GAF图像并结合联邦学习与CNN，可在异构IoT设备（包括Raspberry Pi）上实现95.18%准确率的隐私保护心电分类，兼顾性能和通信/资源效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在IoT医疗场景中，隐私和数据主权至关重要；传统集中式训练需要上传敏感医疗数据到云端，不利于隐私保护。将ECG信号转换为GAF图像便于CNN高效特征提取；联邦学习能在保持数据不出本地的前提下实现模型训练，适合异构IoT设备部署。

Method: 将1D ECG信号转换为2D Gramian Angular Field（GAF）图像，使用CNN作为本地模型，并在联邦学习框架下多设备协同训练（Server/Laptop/Raspberry Pi 4）。评估指标包括分类准确率、训练时间、通信开销和资源利用。与单客户端基线比较以验证FL的优势。

Result: 多客户端FL-GAF模型在实验中达到了95.18%的分类准确率，训练时间优于单客户端基线，并在通信开销和资源利用方面表现高效。Raspberry Pi 4等资源受限设备能够承担GAF转换和本地训练，验证了方法在异构设备上的可行性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出将1D心电信号转换为2D GAF图像，并在联邦学习框架中使用CNN进行分类，从而在IoT医疗环境中实现隐私保护的心电分类。实验在服务器、笔记本和Raspberry Pi 4上部署，结果显示多客户端FL-GAF模型在准确率（95.18%）和训练时间上显著优于单客户端基线，同时在通信和资源利用上保持高效。总体结论是：GAF结合FL在资源受限边缘设备上可行，能实现可扩展且隐私安全的智能健康监测部署。

Abstract: This study presents a federated learning (FL) framework for
privacy-preserving electrocardiogram (ECG) classification in Internet of Things
(IoT) healthcare environments. By transforming 1D ECG signals into 2D Gramian
Angular Field (GAF) images, the proposed approach enables efficient feature
extraction through Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) while ensuring that
sensitive medical data remain local to each device. This work is among the
first to experimentally validate GAF-based federated ECG classification across
heterogeneous IoT devices, quantifying both performance and communication
efficiency. To evaluate feasibility in realistic IoT settings, we deployed the
framework across a server, a laptop, and a resource-constrained Raspberry Pi 4,
reflecting edge-cloud integration in IoT ecosystems. Experimental results
demonstrate that the FL-GAF model achieves a high classification accuracy of
95.18% in a multi-client setup, significantly outperforming a single-client
baseline in both accuracy and training time. Despite the added computational
complexity of GAF transformations, the framework maintains efficient resource
utilization and communication overhead. These findings highlight the potential
of lightweight, privacy-preserving AI for IoT-based healthcare monitoring,
supporting scalable and secure edge deployments in smart health systems.

</details>


### [26] [Laugh, Relate, Engage: Stylized Comment Generation for Short Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03757)
*Xuan Ouyang,Senan Wang,Bouzhou Wang,Siyuan Xiahou,Jinrong Zhou,Yuekang Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出面向短视频的模块化多智能体评论生成系统，支持六种风格与中英双平台，实验证明在风格可控性和用户偏好上具有显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短视频评论在社区参与和内容再创中重要，但生成的评论需同时满足平台合规、风格多样性与上下文相关性，现有方法难以兼顾这些要求，因此提出可控且文化适应性强的评论生成框架。

Method: 系统由视频分段、语境与情感分析、风格感知提示生成等模块组成；利用多模态大模型直接输入视频，使用显式提示标记和少样本示例实现六种评论风格的细粒度控制；并通过官方API构建双语数据集进行训练与评估。

Result: 在自动化指标（原创性、相关性、风格一致性）与大规模人工偏好测试（40视频、105参与者）上，LOLGORITHM在抖音上偏好率超过90%，在YouTube上为87.55%，显著优于基线模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出了LOLGORITHM，一个模块化多智能体系统，用于可控的短视频评论生成，能在风格、多模态处理和平台合规性间取得平衡，实验显示在中英双平台上明显优于基线，能提升用户参与和创意互动。

Abstract: Short-video platforms have become a central medium in the modern Internet
landscape, where efficient information delivery and strong interactivity are
reshaping user engagement and cultural dissemination. Among the various forms
of user interaction, comments play a vital role in fostering community
participation and enabling content re-creation. However, generating comments
that are both compliant with platform guidelines and capable of exhibiting
stylistic diversity and contextual awareness remains a significant challenge.
We introduce LOLGORITHM, a modular multi-agent system (MAS) designed for
controllable short-video comment generation. The system integrates video
segmentation, contextual and affective analysis, and style-aware prompt
construction. It supports six distinct comment styles: puns (homophones),
rhyming, meme application, sarcasm (irony), plain humor, and content
extraction. Powered by a multimodal large language model (MLLM), LOLGORITHM
directly processes video inputs and achieves fine-grained style control through
explicit prompt markers and few-shot examples. To support development and
evaluation, we construct a bilingual dataset using official APIs from Douyin
(Chinese) and YouTube (English), covering five popular video genres: comedy
skits, daily life jokes, funny animal clips, humorous commentary, and talk
shows. Evaluation combines automated metrics originality, relevance, and style
conformity with a large-scale human preference study involving 40 videos and
105 participants. Results show that LOLGORITHM significantly outperforms
baseline models, achieving preference rates of over 90% on Douyin and 87.55% on
YouTube. This work presents a scalable and culturally adaptive framework for

more than 10.5k examples using exclusively new images not found in web training

during training. Among the models we evaluated, we found scale can provide

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实场景中只有部分特征（如年龄、性别）需要隐私保护，全样本DP-SGD导致过多噪声与性能下降，需提升特征级隐私-效用平衡。

Result: 在PhysioNet的脓毒症预测与MIMIC-III临床笔记分类任务中，相较于现有隐私保护基线，FusionDP在维持严格特征级隐私的同时显著提升了模型性能。

Abstract: Ensuring the privacy of sensitive training data is crucial in
privacy-preserving machine learning. However, in practical scenarios, privacy

to their re-identification potential, whereas raw lab results are generally
less sensitive. Traditional DP-SGD enforces privacy protection on all features
in one sample, leading to excessive noise injection and significant utility
degradation. We propose FusionDP, a two-step framework that enhances model
utility under feature-level differential privacy. First, FusionDP leverages

features, treating them as external priors that provide high-quality estimates

training. Second, we introduce a modified DP-SGD algorithm that trains models
on both original and imputed features while formally preserving the privacy of
the original sensitive features. We evaluate FusionDP on two modalities: a
sepsis prediction task on tabular data from PhysioNet and a clinical note
classification task from MIMIC-III. By comparing against privacy-preserving
baselines, our results show that FusionDP significantly improves model
performance while maintaining rigorous feature-level privacy, demonstrating the
potential of foundation model-driven imputation to enhance the privacy-utility
trade-off for various modalities.

### [30] [Fair and Explainable Credit-Scoring under Concept Drift: Adaptive Explanation Frameworks for Evolving Populations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03807)
*Shivogo John*

Motivation: Static explainability techniques (e.g., SHAP) assume fixed data distributions and become unstable or unfair when concept drift occurs in evolving credit systems, necessitating adaptive explanation frameworks to preserve interpretability and fairness.

modern credit-scoring systems. Conventional explainability techniques, such as
SHAP, assume static data and fixed background distributions, making their
explanations unstable and potentially unfair when concept drift occurs. This
study addresses that challenge by developing adaptive explanation frameworks
that recalibrate interpretability and fairness in dynamically evolving credit
models. Using a multi-year credit dataset, we integrate predictive modeling via
XGBoost with three adaptive SHAP variants: (A) per-slice explanation

proxy-variable detection, confirm the resilience of adaptive explanations under
real-world drift conditions. These findings establish adaptive explainability
as a practical mechanism for sustaining transparency, accountability, and
ethical reliability in data-driven credit systems, and more broadly, in any

### [32] [One Size Does Not Fit All: Architecture-Aware Adaptive Batch Scheduling with DEBA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03809)
*François Belias,Naser Ezzati-Jivan,Foutse Khomh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 批量大小自适应并非通用策略，DEBA 展示了面向架构的自适应能显著加速并提升部分网络的性能；利用梯度稳定性指标可预测收益，滑动窗口与足够冷却期是成功要素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑现有自适应批量大小方法“一刀切”的假设，验证不同架构对批量自适应的响应差异并寻找可预测性特征。

Method: 提出 DEBA 调度器，基于监测梯度方差、梯度范数变化与损失变化做批次大小调整；使用滑动窗口统计与冷却期机制进行稳健决策。

Result: 在 CIFAR-10/100 上对六种架构、每种配置多个随机种子进行系统评估：MobileNet-V3、DenseNet-121、EfficientNet-B0 提升训练速度45-62%并提高精度1-7%；ResNet-18 精度+2.4-4.0%、速度+36-43%；ResNet-50 表现不稳；ViT-B16 速度仅+6%且精度维持。滑动窗口与>=5 epoch 冷却期为关键设计。

Conclusion: Adaptive batch size 框架并非对所有架构通用，DEBA 在轻量/中等深度网络上效果显著，但在深层残差网络上不稳定；通过梯度稳定性指标可预测适应性收益。

Abstract: Adaptive batch size methods aim to accelerate neural network training, but
existing approaches apply identical adaptation strategies across all
architectures, assuming a one-size-fits-all solution. We introduce DEBA
(Dynamic Efficient Batch Adaptation), an adaptive batch scheduler that monitors
gradient variance, gradient norm variation and loss variation to guide batch
size adaptations. Through systematic evaluation across six architectures
(ResNet-18/50, DenseNet-121, EfficientNet-B0, MobileNet-V3, ViT-B16) on
CIFAR-10 and CIFAR-100, with five random seeds per configuration, we
demonstrate that the architecture fundamentally determines adaptation efficacy.
Our findings reveal that: (1) lightweight and medium-depth architectures
(MobileNet-V3, DenseNet-121, EfficientNet-B0) achieve a 45-62% training speedup
with simultaneous accuracy improvements of 1-7%; (2) shallow residual networks
(ResNet-18) show consistent gains of +2.4 - 4.0% in accuracy, 36 - 43% in
speedup, while deep residual networks (ResNet-50) exhibit high variance and
occasional degradation; (3) already-stable architectures (ViT-B16) show minimal
speedup (6%) despite maintaining accuracy, indicating that adaptation benefits
vary with baseline optimization characteristics. We introduce a baseline
characterization framework using gradient stability metrics (stability score,
gradient norm variation) that predicts which architectures will benefit from
adaptive scheduling. Our ablation studies reveal critical design choices often
overlooked in prior work: sliding window statistics (vs. full history) and
sufficient cooldown periods (5+ epochs) between adaptations are essential for
success. This work challenges the prevailing assumption that adaptive methods
generalize across architectures and provides the first systematic evidence that
batch size adaptation requires an architecture-aware design.

### [33] [Sketch-Augmented Features Improve Learning Long-Range Dependencies in Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03824)
*Ryien Hosseini,Filippo Simini,Venkatram Vishwanath,Rebecca Willett,Henry Hoffmann*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统GNN基于局部消息传递，虽然有效利用稀疏性与归纳偏置，但在捕获长程依赖时存在oversquashing、节点表示趋同（oversmoothing）与表达力不足等三大挑战。研究旨在通过引入全局、随机且距离敏感的特征来克服这些限制。

Method: 设计并生成唯一、与距离相关且与拓扑无关的随机全局嵌入（Sketched Random Features），将其作为节点特征的补充注入到标准GNN中；通过理论分析说明这些嵌入如何保留长程依赖并防止信息压缩和均化；在多项真实图数据集上与基线和位置编码方法进行对比实验证明其有效性。

Result: 在多个真实世界图学习任务上，注入SRF的GNN在性能上持续优于基础GNN，同时可与图位置编码等现有方法互补，源码公开。

Conclusion: Sketched Random Features（SRF）通过向GNN注入随机化的全局节点嵌入，缓解了长程信息的oversquashing、表示的oversmoothing以及模型表达力受限的问题，显著提升了GNN在实证任务的表现。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks learn on graph-structured data by iteratively
aggregating local neighborhood information. While this local message passing
paradigm imparts a powerful inductive bias and exploits graph sparsity, it also
yields three key challenges: (i) oversquashing of long-range information, (ii)
oversmoothing of node representations, and (iii) limited expressive power. In
this work we inject randomized global embeddings of node features, which we
term \textit{Sketched Random Features}, into standard GNNs, enabling them to
efficiently capture long-range dependencies. The embeddings are unique,
distance-sensitive, and topology-agnostic -- properties which we analytically
and empirically show alleviate the aforementioned limitations when injected
into GNNs. Experimental results on real-world graph learning tasks confirm that
this strategy consistently improves performance over baseline GNNs, offering
both a standalone solution and a complementary enhancement to existing
techniques such as graph positional encodings. Our source code is available at
\href{https://github.com/ryienh/sketched-random-features}{https://github.com/ryienh/sketched-random-features}.

### [34] [From Static to Dynamic: Enhancing Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning via Energy-Guided Diffusion Stratification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03828)
*Lipeng Zu,Hansong Zhou,Xiaonan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出StratDiff：用扩散模型+能量函数生成并评估离线样本相似度，通过KL分层训练，改进离线到在线的RL微调，实验证明优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线到在线RL存在行为策略分布漂移，现有方法很少显式评估或利用离线数据的分布结构，缺乏对不同样本类型自适应的学习策略。

Method: 使用扩散模型学习离线动作先验，再用能量函数修正以提高模仿精度；对每个样本计算生成动作与采样动作的KL散度以分层（离线样本/在线样本），分别采用离线目标和在线学习策略更新；与Cal-QL和IQL结合并在D4RL上评估。

Result: 在D4RL基准上，StratDiff显著优于现有方法，提升了适应性并在多种RL设置下表现更稳定。

Conclusion: StratDiff通过扩散模型+能量函数刻画离线数据分布并据此分层训练，能在离线到在线RL转换中实现更平滑、稳定的策略微调。

Abstract: Transitioning from offline to online reinforcement learning (RL) poses
critical challenges due to distributional shifts between the fixed behavior
policy in the offline dataset and the evolving policy during online learning.
Although this issue is widely recognized, few methods attempt to explicitly
assess or utilize the distributional structure of the offline data itself,
leaving a research gap in adapting learning strategies to different types of
samples. To address this challenge, we propose an innovative method,
Energy-Guided Diffusion Stratification (StratDiff), which facilitates smoother
transitions in offline-to-online RL. StratDiff deploys a diffusion model to
learn prior knowledge from the offline dataset. It then refines this knowledge
through energy-based functions to improve policy imitation and generate
offline-like actions during online fine-tuning. The KL divergence between the
generated action and the corresponding sampled action is computed for each
sample and used to stratify the training batch into offline-like and
online-like subsets. Offline-like samples are updated using offline objectives,
while online-like samples follow online learning strategies. We demonstrate the
effectiveness of StratDiff by integrating it with off-the-shelf methods Cal-QL
and IQL. Extensive empirical evaluations on D4RL benchmarks show that StratDiff
significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving enhanced adaptability and
more stable performance across diverse RL settings.

Abstract: Causal structure learning has long been the central task of inferring causal

higher-order mechanisms, however, an explicit treatment of interactions in
causal discovery has received little attention. In this work, we focus on
extending the causal additive model (CAM) to additive models with higher-order
interactions. This second level of modularity we introduce to the structure
learning problem is most easily represented by a directed acyclic hypergraph
which extends the DAG. We introduce the necessary definitions and theoretical
tools to handle the novel structure we introduce and then provide

equivalence classes. We next provide insights into why learning the more
complex hypergraph structure may actually lead to better empirical results. In
particular, more restrictive assumptions like CAM correspond to easier-to-learn
hyper DAGs and better finite sample complexity. We finally develop an extension
of the greedy CAM algorithm which can handle the more complex hyper DAG search
space and demonstrate its empirical usefulness in synthetic experiments.

*Lipeng Zu,Hansong Zhou,Xiaonan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SADQ通过建模随机转移并将后继状态分布整合进Q更新，减少因历史样本导致的更新方差，提升训练稳定性与效率；理论与实验证据均支持其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DQN目标更新依赖于来自重放缓冲区的、生成自历史（可能次优）策略的下一状态，导致学习信号不足并引入高方差，尤其当样本与当前策略不匹配时问题加剧。

Method: 构建一个随机化的转移模型以估计后继状态分布，并在Q值更新中用该分布进行期望化处理；基于该模型设计更高效的动作选择策略；理论上证明所提方法在保持无偏性同时能降低训练方差。

Result: 理论证明SADQ保持无偏估计并减少更新方差；在多项标准基准与真实矢量控制任务上，SADQ在稳定性和学习效率上均显著优于DQN及变体。

Conclusion: SADQ通过对环境变换建模并将后继状态分布整合进Q估计，缓解了因重放缓存中旧策略样本导致的高方差与不稳定问题，从而提升训练稳定性与效率。

Abstract: Deep Q-Networks (DQNs) estimate future returns by learning from transitions
sampled from a replay buffer. However, the target updates in DQN often rely on
next states generated by actions from past, potentially suboptimal, policy. As
a result, these states may not provide informative learning signals, causing
high variance into the update process. This issue is exacerbated when the
sampled transitions are poorly aligned with the agent's current policy. To
address this limitation, we propose the Successor-state Aggregation Deep
Q-Network (SADQ), which explicitly models environment dynamics using a
stochastic transition model. SADQ integrates successor-state distributions into
the Q-value estimation process, enabling more stable and policy-aligned value
updates. Additionally, it explores a more efficient action selection strategy
with the modeled transition structure. We provide theoretical guarantees that
SADQ maintains unbiased value estimates while reducing training variance. Our
extensive empirical results across standard RL benchmarks and real-world
vector-based control tasks demonstrate that SADQ consistently outperforms DQN
variants in both stability and learning efficiency.

</details>


### [37] [Benchmark Datasets for Lead-Lag Forecasting on Social Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03877)
*Kimia Kazemian,Zhenzhen Liu,Yangfanyu Yang,Katie Z Luo,Shuhan Gu,Audrey Du,Xinyu Yang,Jack Jansons,Kilian Q Weinberger,John Thickstun,Yian Yin,Sarah Dean*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Lead-Lag Forecasting问题，发布arXiv和GitHub两个大规模基准数据集，验证并基准化方法，推动对早期使用行为预测滞后影响的系统研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交与协作平台常产生早期交互（浏览、点赞、下载）与滞后结果（引用、销量、评论）之间的时间偏移关联，但缺乏标准化数据集与统一问题定义，阻碍了该类问题在时间序列社区的发展。

Method: 构建并公开两个大规模基准数据集（arXiv：访问量->引用，GitHub：pushes/stars->forks），对数据进行清洗与文档化；通过统计检验与分类实验证实存在lead-lag关系；对若干参数和非参数回归基线方法进行基准测试。

Result: 提供了覆盖多年长期动态且避免幸存者偏差的高容量数据集，验证了lead-lag动态的存在并报告了基线模型性能，为LLF的系统研究提供了实证基础和可复现资源（数据门户已公开）。

Conclusion: 本文提出并确立了Lead-Lag Forecasting (LLF)作为一个统一的时间序列预测范式，展示了早期使用行为可以预测滞后出现的更高影响事件。

Abstract: Social and collaborative platforms emit multivariate time-series traces in
which early interactions-such as views, likes, or downloads-are followed,
sometimes months or years later, by higher impact like citations, sales, or
reviews. We formalize this setting as Lead-Lag Forecasting (LLF): given an
early usage channel (the lead), predict a correlated but temporally shifted
outcome channel (the lag). Despite the ubiquity of such patterns, LLF has not
been treated as a unified forecasting problem within the time-series community,
largely due to the absence of standardized datasets. To anchor research in LLF,
here we present two high-volume benchmark datasets-arXiv (accesses -> citations
of 2.3M papers) and GitHub (pushes/stars -> forks of 3M repositories)-and
outline additional domains with analogous lead-lag dynamics, including
Wikipedia (page views -> edits), Spotify (streams -> concert attendance),
e-commerce (click-throughs -> purchases), and LinkedIn profile (views ->
messages). Our datasets provide ideal testbeds for lead-lag forecasting, by
capturing long-horizon dynamics across years, spanning the full spectrum of
outcomes, and avoiding survivorship bias in sampling. We documented all
technical details of data curation and cleaning, verified the presence of
lead-lag dynamics through statistical and classification tests, and benchmarked
parametric and non-parametric baselines for regression. Our study establishes
LLF as a novel forecasting paradigm and lays an empirical foundation for its
systematic exploration in social and usage data. Our data portal with downloads
and documentation is available at https://lead-lag-forecasting.github.io/.

</details>


### [38] [DecoHD: Decomposed Hyperdimensional Classification under Extreme Memory Budgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03911)
*Sanggeon Yun,Hyunwoo Oh,Ryozo Masukawa,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DecoHD 通过学习的分解 HDC 参数化在极小内存下保持高精度与鲁棒性，并显著提高硬件能效与速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 HDC 在缩减特征或类别维度时会损失集中性与鲁棒性，且现有分解方法使用固定原子超向量不适合压缩可学习的类别原型，因此需新的分解学习策略。

Method: 提出将 HDC 原型分解为每层共享的小通道集合，采用层间乘性绑定与最终的 bundling 头以在紧凑因子中构建大表示；训练端到端，推理保留纯 HDC 操作。

Result: 在多个评估中，DecoHD 在极端内存约束下仅有微小精度下降（平均 0.1-0.15%，最差 5.7%），对随机位翻转更鲁棒，训练参数数目可减少约 97%，硬件上相对 CPU/GPU/HDC ASIC 分别有显著能耗与速度提升。

Conclusion: DecoHD 在保持 HDC 原生操作的同时，通过分解参数化实现极高的压缩率与较小的精度损失，提升了鲁棒性并带来显著硬件能效/速度优势。

Abstract: Decomposition is a proven way to shrink deep networks without changing I/O.
We bring this idea to hyperdimensional computing (HDC), where footprint cuts
usually shrink the feature axis and erode concentration and robustness. Prior
HDC decompositions decode via fixed atomic hypervectors, which are ill-suited
for compressing learned class prototypes. We introduce DecoHD, which learns
directly in a decomposed HDC parameterization: a small, shared set of per-layer
channels with multiplicative binding across layers and bundling at the end,
yielding a large representational space from compact factors. DecoHD compresses
along the class axis via a lightweight bundling head while preserving native
bind-bundle-score; training is end-to-end, and inference remains pure HDC,
aligning with in/near-memory accelerators. In evaluation, DecoHD attains
extreme memory savings with only minor accuracy degradation under tight
deployment budgets. On average it stays within about 0.1-0.15% of a strong
non-reduced HDC baseline (worst case 5.7%), is more robust to random bit-flip
noise, reaches its accuracy plateau with up to ~97% fewer trainable parameters,
and -- in hardware -- delivers roughly 277x/35x energy/speed gains over a CPU
(AMD Ryzen 9 9950X), 13.5x/3.7x over a GPU (NVIDIA RTX 4090), and 2.0x/2.4x
over a baseline HDC ASIC.

</details>

First, to improve predictive accuracy while retaining interpretability, we

improve prediction of age, gender, income, and household structure over

planners to quantify uncertainty. Third, to improve generalization and sample

limited or when applying models across different time periods (i.e., when the

### [40] [SynQuE: Estimating Synthetic Dataset Quality Without Annotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03928)
*Arthur Chen,Victor Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出SynQuE框架和基准，通过嵌入度量与LENS（LLM推理）构建代理，实现仅用有限无标签真实数据也能有效挑选合成数据，提升多任务上真实性能，LENS在复杂任务上尤为有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真实数据稀缺（成本或隐私）场景下，需要有效选择合成数据以提升真实任务性能。

Method: 构建综合基准并引入代理度量（基于分布和多样性，利用嵌入模型适配），以及针对复杂任务提出LENS——一种基于大语言模型推理的新代理。

Result: 在多个任务（情感分析、Text2SQL、网页导航、图像分类）上，SynQuE代理与真实任务性能相关；LENS在复杂规划任务上表现最佳。以Text-to-SQL为例，通过SynQuE选择的top-3合成数据集将准确率从30.4%提升到38.4%（+8.1%）。

Conclusion: 作者提出并形式化了SynQuE问题，即在仅有有限无标签真实数据时，依据预计的真实任务性能对合成数据集进行排序。

Abstract: We introduce and formalize the Synthetic Dataset Quality Estimation (SynQuE)
problem: ranking synthetic datasets by their expected real-world task
performance using only limited unannotated real data. This addresses a critical
and open challenge where data is scarce due to collection costs or privacy
constraints. We establish the first comprehensive benchmarks for this problem
by introducing and evaluating proxy metrics that choose synthetic data for
training to maximize task performance on real data. We introduce the first
proxy metrics for SynQuE by adapting distribution and diversity-based distance
measures to our context via embedding models. To address the shortcomings of
these metrics on complex planning tasks, we propose LENS, a novel proxy that
leverages large language model reasoning. Our results show that SynQuE proxies
correlate with real task performance across diverse tasks, including sentiment
analysis, Text2SQL, web navigation, and image classification, with LENS
consistently outperforming others on complex tasks by capturing nuanced
characteristics. For instance, on text-to-SQL parsing, training on the top-3
synthetic datasets selected via SynQuE proxies can raise accuracy from 30.4% to
38.4 (+8.1)% on average compared to selecting data indiscriminately. This work
establishes SynQuE as a practical framework for synthetic data selection under
real-data scarcity and motivates future research on foundation model-based data
characterization and fine-grained data selection.

### [42] [LogHD: Robust Compression of Hyperdimensional Classifiers via Logarithmic Class-Axis Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03938)
*Sanggeon Yun,Hyunwoo Oh,Ryozo Masukawa,Pietro Mercati,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出LogHD，通过在类别轴进行对数压缩把类别原型数从C降至≈log_k C以节省O(D log_k C)存储，保持高维鲁棒性并提升抗噪性；实验证明在相同内存下对比特翻转更鲁棒，并在ASIC上显著提高能效与速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准HDC每类一个原型导致内存随类别数线性增长，受内存、能耗和可靠性约束的系统需要更紧凑的表示而不牺牲鲁棒性，因此探索在类别轴做对数压缩以节省存储并提高抗错误率。

Method: 提出将类别原型按字母表大小k编码为n≈⌈log_k C⌉个捆绑向量，使用容量感知码本(capacity-aware codebook)和基于剖面(profile-based)的解码方法，在保持维度D不变的同时减少类别轴存储；并与特征轴稀疏化配合。实现包括算法细节、抗噪实验以及ASIC硬件实现并与CPU/GPU及baseline ASIC比较性能。

Result: LogHD在多个数据集与注入比特翻转实验中，在相同内存成本下达到与常规模型竞争的精度且在容错性上优于特征轴压缩；ASIC实现在能耗和吞吐量上优于高端CPU/GPU，并相较于特征轴HDC ASIC基线能效高4.06×，速度快2.19×。

Conclusion: LogHD通过在类别轴上做对数级压缩，把每类的原型向量替换为约n≈⌈log_k C⌉个捆绑超向量，并在n维激活空间解码，从而把内存复杂度从O(CD)降为O(D log_k C)，同时保持高维D以维持鲁棒性。实验表明，在相同内存下，LogHD在抗比特翻转噪声方面比特征轴压缩能承受约2.5-3.0倍更高的错误率；ASIC实现相比高端CPU/GPU显著提升能效和速度，并比特征轴HDC ASIC基线更高效、更快。

Abstract: Hyperdimensional computing (HDC) suits memory, energy, and
reliability-constrained systems, yet the standard "one prototype per class"
design requires $O(CD)$ memory (with $C$ classes and dimensionality $D$). Prior
compaction reduces $D$ (feature axis), improving storage/compute but weakening
robustness. We introduce LogHD, a logarithmic class-axis reduction that
replaces the $C$ per-class prototypes with $n\!\approx\!\lceil\log_k C\rceil$
bundle hypervectors (alphabet size $k$) and decodes in an $n$-dimensional
activation space, cutting memory to $O(D\log_k C)$ while preserving $D$. LogHD
uses a capacity-aware codebook and profile-based decoding, and composes with
feature-axis sparsification. Across datasets and injected bit flips, LogHD
attains competitive accuracy with smaller models and higher resilience at
matched memory. Under equal memory, it sustains target accuracy at roughly
$2.5$-$3.0\times$ higher bit-flip rates than feature-axis compression; an ASIC
instantiation delivers $498\times$ energy efficiency and $62.6\times$ speedup
over an AMD Ryzen 9 9950X and $24.3\times$/$6.58\times$ over an NVIDIA RTX
4090, and is $4.06\times$ more energy-efficient and $2.19\times$ faster than a
feature-axis HDC ASIC baseline.

</details>

Abstract: Differentially private in-context learning (DP-ICL) has recently become an

manner. Our method outperforms existing baselines by a substantial margin

database of context data, combined with a privacy filter that tracks the
cumulative privacy cost of selected samples to ensure adherence to a central
differential privacy budget. Experimental results on text classification and
document question answering show a clear advantage of the proposed method over
existing baselines.

Motivation: 随着LLM能力和应用场景的扩展，传统文本为主的RLHF不足以覆盖多模态反馈、文化差异与低延迟场景的需求，因此需要系统梳理新兴对齐方法与挑战，指导更稳健与公平的模型部署。

Method: 论文通过回顾与比较现有算法（PPO、DPO、GRPO），并在多模态对齐、文化公平与低延迟优化三个维度进行系统综述，综合实验结果与理论分析，提出对比分析与未来研究路线图。

Result: 总结最新进展，指出多模态对齐需解决跨模态标注一致性与架构适配，文化公平需建立多语种多文化基准和公平性度量，低延迟优化需在在线学习与样本效率间取得平衡；同时提供一系列研究建议与开放问题。

Conclusion: 本文归纳表明，RLHF仍为对齐LLM的基石，但研究正向多模态对齐、文化公平与低延迟优化扩展。尽管现有方法（如PPO、DPO、GRPO）各有优劣，结合多模态反馈与公正性约束的混合框架更有潜力，但仍需在标注质量、跨文化评价基准、样本效率和实时性上攻关。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) is the standard for
aligning Large Language Models (LLMs), yet recent progress has moved beyond
canonical text-based methods. This survey synthesizes the new frontier of

cultural fairness, and low-latency optimization. To systematically explore

### [45] [Conditional Score Learning for Quickest Change Detection in Markov Transition Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03953)
*Wuxia Chen,Taposh Banerjee,Vahid Tarokh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过直接学习条件得分并构造截断的Hyvärinen得分差CUSUM统计，本文在高维未知转移核的马尔可夫模型中实现了有理论保证的最速变更检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维马尔可夫过程的最速变更检测中，传统方法依赖完整似然或转移核的显式计算，难以在高维或未知转移核场景下应用。直接学习条件得分函数可以避免估计完整似然，提供一种可行且可扩展的检测方法。

Method: 1) 从样本对(x,y)直接估计条件得分函数∇_y log p(y|x)。2) 构造基于条件Hyvärinen得分差的CUSUM统计量用于变点检测。3) 为使增量有界，引入截断（truncation）统计量。4) 在均匀遍历马氏链上应用Hoeffding不等式，推导虚警时间的指数下界并证明检测延迟的渐近上界。

Result: 提出并分析了基于条件得分的CUSUM方法：在理论上给出虚警率（平均虚警时间）呈指数级增长的下界和检测延迟的渐近上界；在实践上方法避免显式似然计算，适用于高维数据。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于条件得分函数的CUSUM检测方法，通过直接从样本对(x,y)学习条件得分∇_y log p(y|x)，绕过显式似然计算，从而实现高维马尔可夫过程转移核突变的检测。通过截断统计量保证增量有界，利用均匀遍历性下的Hoeffding不等式，证明了虚警时间的指数下界及检测延迟的渐近上界，兼顾理论保证与可行性。

Abstract: We address the problem of quickest change detection in Markov processes with
unknown transition kernels. The key idea is to learn the conditional score
$\nabla_{\mathbf{y}} \log p(\mathbf{y}|\mathbf{x})$ directly from sample pairs
$( \mathbf{x},\mathbf{y})$, where both $\mathbf{x}$ and $\mathbf{y}$ are
high-dimensional data generated by the same transition kernel. In this way, we
avoid explicit likelihood evaluation and provide a practical way to learn the
transition dynamics. Based on this estimation, we develop a score-based CUSUM
procedure that uses conditional Hyvarinen score differences to detect changes
in the kernel. To ensure bounded increments, we propose a truncated version of
the statistic. With Hoeffding's inequality for uniformly ergodic Markov
processes, we prove exponential lower bounds on the mean time to false alarm.
We also prove asymptotic upper bounds on detection delay. These results give
both theoretical guarantees and practical feasibility for score-based detection
in high-dimensional Markov models.

</details>


### [46] [PrivacyCD: Hierarchical Unlearning for Protecting Student Privacy in Cognitive Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03966)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着用户“被遗忘权”意识增强，需从CD模型中移除特定学生数据，但现有CD模型缺乏有效数据删除机制，通用删除算法在CD场景中效果不佳。

Method: 提出HIF算法，基于观察到CD模型参数重要性具有层级化、层间差异的特性，设计了一种平滑机制，将个体参数重要性与层级重要性相结合，从而精确识别需遗忘数据对应的参数并进行处理。

Result: 在三个真实数据集上的实验显示，HIF在关键指标上显著优于基线方法，兼顾删除效果、模型性能和计算效率，首次为CD模型提供了有效的数据删除方案。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了针对认知诊断（CD）模型的数据“遗忘”问题的首个系统性研究，提出了层次重要性引导遗忘（HIF）算法，能更有效地区分与需删除数据相关的参数，从而在删除完整性、模型效用与效率之间取得更好平衡。

Abstract: The need to remove specific student data from cognitive diagnosis (CD) models
has become a pressing requirement, driven by users' growing assertion of their
"right to be forgotten". However, existing CD models are largely designed
without privacy considerations and lack effective data unlearning mechanisms.
Directly applying general purpose unlearning algorithms is suboptimal, as they
struggle to balance unlearning completeness, model utility, and efficiency when
confronted with the unique heterogeneous structure of CD models. To address
this, our paper presents the first systematic study of the data unlearning
problem for CD models, proposing a novel and efficient algorithm: hierarchical
importanceguided forgetting (HIF). Our key insight is that parameter importance
in CD models exhibits distinct layer wise characteristics. HIF leverages this
via an innovative smoothing mechanism that combines individual and layer, level
importance, enabling a more precise distinction of parameters associated with
the data to be unlearned. Experiments on three real world datasets show that
HIF significantly outperforms baselines on key metrics, offering the first
effective solution for CD models to respond to user data removal requests and
for deploying high-performance, privacy preserving AI systems

### [47] [Non-Asymptotic Optimization and Generalization Bounds for Stochastic Gauss-Newton in Overparameterized Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.03972)
*Semih Cayci*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文证明了带LM阻尼和小批量采样的随机Gauss-Newton方法在过参数化网络上既有有限时间收敛性也有一致稳定性导出的泛化界，表明沿优化路径更大的Gauss-Newton最小特征值可以提升泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高阶优化方法（如Gauss-Newton）如何影响深度学习模型的泛化性能，特别是在过参数化模型和小批量随机训练下，理解曲率信息在优化与泛化之间的作用。

Method: 作者采用参数空间的变度量分析（variable-metric analysis）证明有限时间收敛界，显式给出收敛率对批大小、网络宽度与深度的依赖；并基于一致稳定性（uniform stability）技术，结合过参数化假设，推导了SGN的非渐近泛化界，刻画了曲率（Gauss-Newton矩阵特征值）、批量大小和过参数化程度对泛化的影响。

Result: 结果包括：1）在一定条件下给出SGN的有限时间收敛界，且界中包含对批大小、网络深度和宽度的显式依赖；2）给出基于一致稳定性的非渐近泛化界，显示更大Gauss-Newton最小特征值沿路径会缩紧稳定性界，从而有利于泛化；3）识别出SGN有利的泛化区间，其中曲率有利于稳定性与泛化。

Conclusion: 该论文结论是：在过参数化深度神经网络的回归问题中，带Levenberg-Marquardt阻尼的随机Gauss-Newton（SGN）方法在有限时间内收敛，并且可以通过一致稳定性得到非渐近的泛化界，表明较大的Gauss-Newton矩阵最小特征值沿优化路径可以带来更好的泛化性。

Abstract: An important question in deep learning is how higher-order optimization
methods affect generalization. In this work, we analyze a stochastic
Gauss-Newton (SGN) method with Levenberg-Marquardt damping and mini-batch
sampling for training overparameterized deep neural networks with smooth
activations in a regression setting. Our theoretical contributions are twofold.
First, we establish finite-time convergence bounds via a variable-metric
analysis in parameter space, with explicit dependencies on the batch size,
network width and depth. Second, we derive non-asymptotic generalization bounds
for SGN using uniform stability in the overparameterized regime, characterizing
the impact of curvature, batch size, and overparameterization on generalization
performance. Our theoretical results identify a favorable generalization regime
for SGN in which a larger minimum eigenvalue of the Gauss-Newton matrix along
the optimization path yields tighter stability bounds.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入关系矩阵建模任务间依赖，将节点与路径相关性编码为图结构先验；在不同层嵌入模块化adapter，采用低秩映射与可插拔机制实现跨任务组合与重用；基于结构先验进行路径选择与权重分配，减少路径冲突与冗余计算；并开展超参、环境与数据敏感性实验验证方法鲁棒性。

Result: 在多项实验（超参数、环境、数据敏感性分析）中，方法在任务预测准确率、adapter权重分配精度和整体计算效率上均显著优于对比方案，同时保持模型轻量化设计，验证了图先验与模块化机制的协同优势。
